HomeStudent::HomeStudent(QWidget *parent) : QDialog(parent), ui(new Ui::HomeStudent)
{
    ui->setupUi(this);
    showMaximized();
    setWindowTitle("CheckerApp");
    QPixmap pix("C:/Users/bianc/OneDrive/Desktop/proiect POO/client/CheckerApp/imageUser.png");
    ui->label_imageUser->setPixmap(pix);

  //ui->label_Username->setText(currentUser->getUserName());

    ui->label->resize(700,700);

    ui->comboBox->addItem("C");
    ui->comboBox->addItem("C++");
    ui->comboBox->addItem("Python");

    connect(ui->comboBox, SIGNAL(currentIndexChanged(int)), this, SLOT(onComboBoxIndexChanged(int)));
}

HomeStudent::~HomeStudent()
{
    delete ui;
}

void HomeStudent::on_pushButton_clicked()
{
    this->hide();
    MainWindow* mainWindow = new MainWindow(this);
    mainWindow->show();
}

void HomeStudent::on_pushButton_5_clicked()
{
    char * buff;
    QString Code = ui->plainTextEdit->toPlainText();
    int TypeCode=ui->comboBox->currentIndex();
    TypeCode+=3;

    if(!Code.isEmpty())
    {
        QByteArray byteCode = Code.toUtf8();

        const char* dataCode = byteCode.constData();

        buff= (char*)malloc(strlen(dataCode) +2);

        strcat(buff, QString::number(TypeCode).toUtf8().constData());
        strcat(buff,"$");
         strcat(buff, byteCode.constData());

       if (ClientConnection::getInstance().sendData(buff)) {
            QString message = "Message sent: " + QString::fromUtf8(buff) + "\n";
            qDebug() << message;
            Logger::getInstance()->log(message.toStdString());
        }

       ui->label_2->setText(ClientConnection::getInstance().receiveDataCompilate());
    }
    free(buff);
}
